(** ** Equivalence of categories

Authors: Benedikt Ahrens, Chris Kapulkin, Mike Shulman (January 2013)

*)


(** ** Contents:

- Definition of (adjoint) equivalence of categories [adj_equivalence_of_cats]
- Constructor for an equivalence of categories from a right adjoint functor
    [adj_equivalence_from_right_adjoint]
- Equivalence of categories yields weak equivalence of object types
    [weq_on_objects_from_adj_equiv_of_cats]
- A fully faithful and ess. surjective functor induces equivalence of precategories if it is also
    split ess. surjective or if the source is a univalent_category
    [rad_equivalence_of_cats'] [rad_equivalence_of_cats]

*)

Local Open Scope cat.

(** * Sloppy equivalence of categories *)

Definition forms_equivalence {A B : category} (X : adjunction_data A B)
           (η := adjunit X) (ε := adjcounit X) : UU
  := (∏ a, is_z_isomorphism (η a)) × (∏ b, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)).

Definition make_forms_equivalence {A B : category}
           (adjData : adjunction_data A B)
           (η := adjunit adjData)
           (ε := adjcounit adjData)
           (η_iso : ∏(a : A), is_z_isomorphism (η a))
           (ε_iso : ∏(b : B), is_z_isomorphism (ε b)) : forms_equivalence adjData
    := (η_iso ,, ε_iso).

Definition equivalence_of_cats (A B : category) : UU
  := ∑ (X : adjunction_data A B), forms_equivalence X.

Coercion adjunction_data_from_equivalence_of_cats {A B}
         (X : equivalence_of_cats A B) : adjunction_data A B := pr1 X.

Definition make_equivalence_of_cats {A B : category}
           (adjData : adjunction_data A B)
           (eqvProp : forms_equivalence adjData) : equivalence_of_cats A B
  := (adjData ,, eqvProp).


A, B: category
X: equivalence_of_cats A B
a: A
z_iso a (right_functor X (left_functor X a))


A, B: category
X: equivalence_of_cats A B
a: A
z_iso a (right_functor X (left_functor X a))

  
A, B: category
X: equivalence_of_cats A B
a: A
is_z_isomorphism (adjunit X a)

  exact (pr1 (pr2 X) a).
Defined.


A, B: category
X: equivalence_of_cats A B
b: B
z_iso (left_functor X (right_functor X b)) b


A, B: category
X: equivalence_of_cats A B
b: B
z_iso (left_functor X (right_functor X b)) b

 
A, B: category
X: equivalence_of_cats A B
b: B
is_z_isomorphism (adjcounit X b)

 exact (pr2 (pr2 X) b).
Defined.

(** * Equivalence of (pre)categories *)

Definition adj_equivalence_of_cats {A B : category} (F : functor A B) : UU :=
   ∑ (H : is_left_adjoint F), forms_equivalence H.

Definition adj_from_equiv (D1 D2 : category) (F : functor D1 D2):
    adj_equivalence_of_cats F → is_left_adjoint F := λ x, pr1 x.
Coercion adj_from_equiv : adj_equivalence_of_cats >-> is_left_adjoint.


A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
G: B ⟶ A
η: functor_identity A ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity B
H1: form_adjunction F G η ε
H2: forms_equivalence (F,, G,, η,, ε)
adj_equivalence_of_cats F

H1: form_adjunction G F η ε
H2: ∏ a : B, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
H3: ∏ a : A, is_z_isomorphism (ε a)
a: A
identity (functor_identity B (F a)) =
(η (F a),, H2 (F a)) · functor_on_z_iso F (ε a,, H3 a)

      
A, B: category

G: B ⟶ A

ε: F ∙ G ⟹ functor_identity A
H1: form_adjunction G F η ε
H2: ∏ a : B, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
H3: ∏ a : A, is_z_isomorphism (ε a)
a: A
(η (F a),, H2 (F a)) · functor_on_z_iso F (ε a,, H3 a) =
identity (functor_identity B (F a))

      apply (pr2 H1).

Definition adj_equivalence_from_right_adjoint
  {A B : category}
  (F : functor A B)
  (H1 : is_right_adjoint F)
  (H2 : ∏ a, is_z_isomorphism ((unit_from_right_adjoint H1) a))
  (H3 : ∏ a, is_z_isomorphism ((counit_from_right_adjoint H1) a))
  : adj_equivalence_of_cats F
  := make_adj_equivalence_of_cats'
    F
    (left_adjoint H1)
    (unit_from_right_adjoint H1)
    (counit_from_right_adjoint H1)
    (pr2 (pr2 H1))
    H2
    H3.

Definition adj_equivalence_inv {A B : category}
  {F : functor A B} (HF : adj_equivalence_of_cats F) : functor B A :=
    right_adjoint HF.

Local Notation "HF ^^-1" := (adj_equivalence_inv  HF)(at level 3).

Section Inverse.

  Context {A B : category}.
  Context (F : functor A B).
  Context (H : adj_equivalence_of_cats F).

  Definition adj_equivalence_of_cats_inv
    : adj_equivalence_of_cats H^^-1
    := adj_equivalence_from_right_adjoint
      (right_adjoint H)
      (is_right_adjoint_right_adjoint H)
      (pr1 (pr2 H))
      (pr2 (pr2 H)).

End Inverse.

Section AdjEquiv.
  Definition adj_equiv (A B : category) : UU
    := ∑ F : functor A B,
        adj_equivalence_of_cats F.

  Coercion left_adjequiv (A B : category)
           (F : adj_equiv A B) : functor A B := pr1 F.

  Coercion adj_equiv_of_cats_from_adj {A B : category}
           (E : adj_equiv A B) : adj_equivalence_of_cats E
    := pr2 E.

(** * Adjointification of a sloppy equivalence *)


(** ** One triangle equality is enough *)

(** Proof ported from Peter Lumsdaine's proof of the analog for displayed categories
    see UniMath/TypeTheory
*)

C, D: category
A: adjunction_data C D
E: forms_equivalence A
triangle_1_statement A → triangle_2_statement A


C, D: category
A: adjunction_data C D
E: forms_equivalence A
triangle_1_statement A → triangle_2_statement A

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
E: forms_equivalence (F,, G,, η,, ε)
triangle_1_statement (F,, G,, η,, ε)
→ triangle_2_statement (F,, G,, η,, ε)

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
Hη: ∏ a : C, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
Hε: ∏ b : D, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)
triangle_1_statement (F,, G,, η,, ε)
→ triangle_2_statement (F,, G,, η,, ε)

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
Hη: ∏ a : C, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
Hε: ∏ b : D, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)
(∏ a : C, # F (η a) · ε (F a) = identity (F a))
→ ∏ b : D, η (G b) · # G (ε b) = identity (G b)

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
Hη: ∏ a : C, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
Hε: ∏ b : D, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)
T1: ∏ a : C, # F (η a) · ε (F a) = identity (F a)
x: D
η (G x) · # G (ε x) = identity (G x)

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
Hη: ∏ a : C, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
Hε: ∏ b : D, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)
T1: ∏ a : C, # F (η a) · ε (F a) = identity (F a)
x: D
etaH: ∏ (x x' : C) (f : C ⟦ x, x' ⟧),
f · η x' = η x · # G (# F f)
η (G x) · # G (ε x) = identity (G x)

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
Hη: ∏ a : C, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
Hε: ∏ b : D, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)
T1: ∏ a : C, # F (η a) · ε (F a) = identity (F a)
x: D
etaH: ∏ (x x' : C) (f : C ⟦ x, x' ⟧),
f · η x' = η x · # G (# F f)
epsH: ∏ (x x' : D) (f : D ⟦ x, x' ⟧),
# F (# G f) · ε x' = ε x · f
η (G x) · # G (ε x) = identity (G x)


  (* Algebraically, this goes as follows:
  η G ; G ε
  = G ε^ ; η^ G ; η G ; G ε ; η G ; G ε          [by inverses, 1]
  = G ε^ ; η^ G ; η G ; η G F G ; G F G ε ; G ε  [by naturality, 2]
  = G ε^ ; η^ G ; η G ; η G F G ; G ε F G ; G ε  [by naturality, 3]
  = G ε^ ; η^ G ; η G ; G F η G ; G ε F G ; G ε  [by naturality, 4]
  = G ε^ ; η^ G ; η G ; G (F η ; ε F ) G ; G ε   [by functoriality, 5]
  = G ε^ ; η^ G ; η G ; G ε                      [by T1, 6]
  = 1                                            [by inverses, 7]
*)

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
Hη: ∏ a : C, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
Hε: ∏ b : D, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)
T1: ∏ a : C, # F (η a) · ε (F a) = identity (F a)
x: D
etaH: ∏ (x x' : C) (f : C ⟦ x, x' ⟧),
f · η x' = η x · # G (# F f)
epsH: ∏ (x x' : D) (f : D ⟦ x, x' ⟧),
# F (# G f) · ε x' = ε x · f
make_weq
  (λ f : C ⟦ G x, functor_identity_data C (pr1 G x) ⟧,
   f · (η (pr1 G x),, Hη (pr1 G x)))
  (z_iso_comp_left_isweq (η (pr1 G x),, Hη (pr1 G x))
     (G x)) (η (G x) · # G (ε x)) =
make_weq
  (λ f : C ⟦ G x, functor_identity_data C (pr1 G x) ⟧,
   f · (η (pr1 G x),, Hη (pr1 G x)))
  (z_iso_comp_left_isweq (η (pr1 G x),, Hη (pr1 G x))
     (G x)) (identity (G x))

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
G: D ⟶ C
η: functor_identity C ⟹ F ∙ G
ε: G ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity D
Hη: ∏ a : C, is_z_isomorphism (η a)
Hε: ∏ b : D, is_z_isomorphism (ε b)
T1: ∏ a : C, # F (η a) · ε (F a) = identity (F a)

epsH: ∏ (x x' : D) (f : D ⟦ x, x' ⟧),
# F (# G f) · ε x' = ε x · f
η (G x) · # G (ε x) · η (pr1 G x) =
identity (G x) · η (pr1 G x)

f · η x' = η x · # G (# F f)
epsH: ∏ (x x' : D) (f : D ⟦ x, x' ⟧),
# F (# G f) · ε x' = ε x · f
i:= inv_from_z_iso (functor_on_z_iso G (ε x,, Hε x)): C ⟦ G (functor_identity D x), G ((G ∙ F) x) ⟧
inv_from_z_iso (functor_on_z_iso G (ε x,, Hε x))
· inv_from_z_iso (η (pr1 G x),, Hη (pr1 G x))
· η (G x) · # G (ε x) · η (pr1 G x) · # G (ε x) =
identity (G x)

i:= inv_from_z_iso (functor_on_z_iso G (ε x,, Hε x)): C ⟦ G (functor_identity D x), G ((G ∙ F) x) ⟧
i':= inv_from_z_iso (η (G x),, Hη (G x)): C ⟦ (F ∙ G) (G x), functor_identity C (G x) ⟧
inv_from_z_iso (functor_on_z_iso G (ε x,, Hε x))
· (inv_from_z_iso (η (pr1 G x),, Hη (pr1 G x))
   · (η (G x)
      · (η (G (F (G x)))
         · (# G (ε (F (G x))) · # G (ε x))))) =
identity (G x)

i':= inv_from_z_iso (η (G x),, Hη (G x)): C ⟦ (F ∙ G) (G x), functor_identity C (G x) ⟧
inv_from_z_iso (functor_on_z_iso G (ε x,, Hε x))
· (inv_from_z_iso (η (pr1 G x),, Hη (pr1 G x))
   · (η (G x) · # G (ε x))) = identity (G x)

   · (η (G x) · # G (ε x))) = ?b

(** ** Adjointification *)

Definition adj_equivalence_of_cats_closed_under_iso
  {A B : category}
  {F G : functor A B}
  (α : @z_iso [A,B] F G)
  (HF : adj_equivalence_of_cats F)
  : adj_equivalence_of_cats G
  := is_left_adjoint_closed_under_iso _ _ α HF ,,
    forms_equivalence_closed_under_iso α HF.

(** * From full faithfullness and ess surj to equivalence *)

(** A fully faithful and ess. surjective functor induces an
   equivalence of precategories, if the source is a
    univalent_category.
*)

Section FullyFaithfulAndSplitEssentiallySurjectiveToEquivalence.

Variables A B : category.
Variable F : functor A B.
Hypothesis HF : fully_faithful F.
Hypothesis HS : split_essentially_surjective F.

(** Definition of a functor which will later be the right adjoint. *)

Definition rad_ob
  : ob B -> ob A
  := split_essentially_surjective_inv_on_obj F HS.

(** Definition of the epsilon transformation *)

Definition rad_eps (b : ob B) : z_iso (F (rad_ob b)) b := pr2 (HS _).

(** The right adjoint on morphisms *)


A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
HF: fully_faithful F
HS: split_essentially_surjective F
b, b': B
g: B ⟦ b, b' ⟧
A ⟦ rad_ob b, rad_ob b' ⟧


A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
HF: fully_faithful F
HS: split_essentially_surjective F
b, b': B
g: B ⟦ b, b' ⟧
A ⟦ rad_ob b, rad_ob b' ⟧

  
A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
HF: fully_faithful F
HS: split_essentially_surjective F
b, b': B
g: B ⟦ b, b' ⟧
epsgebs':= rad_eps b · g
· z_iso_inv_from_z_iso (rad_eps b'): B ⟦ F (rad_ob b), F (rad_ob b') ⟧
A ⟦ rad_ob b, rad_ob b' ⟧

  exact (fully_faithful_inv_hom HF (rad_ob b) _ epsgebs').
Defined.

(** Definition of the eta transformation *)


A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
HF: fully_faithful F
HS: split_essentially_surjective F
a: A
A ⟦ a, rad_ob (F a) ⟧


A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
HF: fully_faithful F
HS: split_essentially_surjective F
a: A
A ⟦ a, rad_ob (F a) ⟧

  
A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
HF: fully_faithful F
HS: split_essentially_surjective F
a: A
epsFa:= inv_from_z_iso (rad_eps (F a)): B ⟦ F a, F (rad_ob (F a)) ⟧
A ⟦ a, rad_ob (F a) ⟧

  exact (fully_faithful_inv_hom HF _ _ epsFa).
Defined.

(** Above data specifies a functor *)

Definition rad_functor_data
  : functor_data B A
  := make_functor_data rad_ob rad_mor.

rad_mor a c (f · g) = rad_mor a b f · rad_mor b c g

  
A, B: category
F: A ⟶ B
HF: fully_faithful F
HS: split_essentially_surjective F
a, b, c: B
f: B ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: B ⟦ b, c ⟧

  (rad_eps a · (f · g) · inv_from_z_iso (rad_eps c)) =
fully_faithful_inv_hom HF (rad_ob a) (rad_ob b)
  (rad_eps a · f · inv_from_z_iso (rad_eps b))
· fully_faithful_inv_hom HF (rad_ob b) (rad_ob c)
    (rad_eps b · g · inv_from_z_iso (rad_eps c))

   · (rad_eps b · g · inv_from_z_iso (rad_eps c)))

(** Eta is natural *)

Ltac inv_functor x y :=
   let H:=fresh in
   set (H:= homotweqinvweq (weq_from_fully_faithful HF x y));
     simpl in H;
     unfold fully_faithful_inv_hom; simpl;
     rewrite H; clear H.

· # F (rad_mor (F (rad_ob b)) b (rad_eps b)) =
# F (identity (rad_ob b))

b: B

· # F (rad_mor (F (rad_ob b)) b (rad_eps b)) =
# F (identity (rad_ob b))

· # F
    (fully_faithful_inv_hom HF (rad_ob (F (rad_ob b)))
       (rad_ob b)
       (rad_eps (F (rad_ob b)) · rad_eps b
        · z_iso_inv_from_z_iso (rad_eps b))) =
# F (identity (rad_ob b))

    apply idpath.
Qed.
